  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_49c5efa5-1616-48fb-a09e-615243b51da3'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText3538918657297159951" style="display:none">"An action-packed adventure involving rivalry, intrigue, love, war and jealousy. The well-written, fast-paced plot moves from one dilemma to another…an exhilarating adventure--a big win for sci-fi and romance fans."-- Kirkus Reviews<br /><br />The brave warrior, Prince Comron Van Laven, lays at death’s door after a near fatal transport crash. His life is in the hands of his mortal enemy who does the unthinkable…she saves him…in so many ways. Together the two must battle for survival against the harsh elements, deadly assassins and vicious animal attacks. But that’s only the beginning of their struggles.<br /><br />Once rescued, they must confront the bitter enmity that exists between their worlds, in addition to the dark family secrets threatening to destroy them. Bound by their deep bond, the two embark on a new odyssey where all forces have turned against them and are seeking their lives. But with the help of some shadowy mercenaries, the two just might make it to the throne of Novoxos to stake their royal claim and defeat their enemies.<br /><br />A fresh guilty-pleasure series, this powerful story is the perfect marriage of science fiction and romance. -- Forward Reviews</span>

<div id="review_1309383220" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1309383220" />
    <a title="Hollie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11216149-hollie"><img alt="Hollie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1392298703p2/11216149.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1309383220?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hollie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hollie" href="/user/show/11216149-hollie">Hollie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11216149-hollie?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11216149-hollie?shelf=awful-cover">awful-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11216149-hollie?shelf=kindle-unlimited">kindle-unlimited</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11216149-hollie?shelf=insta-love">insta-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11216149-hollie?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11216149-hollie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11216149-hollie?shelf=badass-heroine">badass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11216149-hollie?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1309383220" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2779135176826156771">I saw this was offered as a kindle-unlimited and the blurb had me sold. <br/><br/>The pros:<br/>* It was a great story on forbidden love<br/>* An action packed plot<br/>* I liked all of the Sci-Fi aspects offered in this read - the world was defiantly one of a kind and I liked that<br/><br/><br/>The cons:<br/>* The title of this book, and the cover give it no justice at all<br/>* I hated all the characters names but the ones that annoyed me the most were the 2 male leads names. Comron and Crausin - It may just be me, but when I read a book and </span>
  <span id="freeText2779135176826156771" style="display:none">I saw this was offered as a kindle-unlimited and the blurb had me sold. <br /><br />The pros:<br />* It was a great story on forbidden love<br />* An action packed plot<br />* I liked all of the Sci-Fi aspects offered in this read - the world was defiantly one of a kind and I liked that<br /><br /><br />The cons:<br />* The title of this book, and the cover give it no justice at all<br />* I hated all the characters names but the ones that annoyed me the most were the 2 male leads names. Comron and Crausin - It may just be me, but when I read a book and 2 of the main characters have a name that start and end with the same letter, it throws me off. I read really fast, so I kept having to go back and assure which character said what, etc. <br />* Comron was rough at times with the heroine. He wasn’t physically violent towards her in the sense of hitting her but the constant grabbing, and aggressive behavior had me losing respect for him. He "grabbed" her quite a few times where she expressed it hurting. Ummmm no. Plus he was overly forceful during sex, sometimes she liked it, but other times she made comments about it not being pleasant. At one time he even mentioned that now that they were together, he was going to have to teach her to "meet his needs" in the bedroom. Hell, she was already giving him some on a regular basis, sometimes at her own expense but he wanted it to be more hostile? Again, No. This made his character come across as very selfish to me. During sex he only seemed concerned with himself - It didn’t have that hot passion feel to it but instead him being overly demanding and showing no concern for the heroines needs.<br />* The father and son (Comron and Crausin) shared their women - some was through a mental link, but others were straight up menages.......and our "hero" liked his sex to pretty much to be violent and rough......just the thought of a father and son sharing women grossed me the fuck out. <br />* The ending left much to be desire - I found it unsatisfying.<br /><br />Overall, I still enjoyed this book. I did like the writing style even though I wasn’t a fan of the hero. The word building, character depth, and storyline execution was very well done. It did have an insta-love feel to it, but in the end I did like the hero and heroine as a couple. Ill still check out the next book in this series.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2779135176826156771" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText13514207440856541437" style="display:none">This author has a captivating style of writing that grabs you from the beginning and has you hurling through the pages to continue the essence of this thrilling odyssey. The author expresses her writing talent with such vividness and finesse, it almost seems as if she's at the scene and simply writing down the events as they occur. As mysterious events are unraveled throughout the story, you begin to view the elements of love and commitment from a different perspective. You become so engulfed in the story and the world she's created, that you begin to ask yourself, if this really is a fictitious story, could love be so dangerous, is it that far from reality?<br /><br />Definitely a must read!</span>

<div id="review_1045318450" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1045318450" />
    <a title="Kristine Pierce" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15186965-kristine-pierce"><img alt="Kristine Pierce" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442650153p2/15186965.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1045318450?book_show_action=true">Sep 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristine Pierce" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristine Pierce" href="/user/show/15186965-kristine-pierce">Kristine Pierce</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23119393-van-laven-chronicles">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15186965-kristine-pierce?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1045318450" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12199650786798441203">“Throne of Novoxos” had me glued to my bed for hours. As I kept turning the pages, I was drawn to another world beyond your regular science fiction. I love the fact that it’s more than that - it’s a hodge podge of topics ranging from Sci-fi, Romance, Action, Adventure, Suspense, Space Travel, Extrasensory powers.<br/><br/>Tyler Chase definitely hit the spot with this one! Such brilliant writing! The descriptions and dialogues are so well written I felt like I was right in the middle of the scenes watching</span>
  <span id="freeText12199650786798441203" style="display:none">“Throne of Novoxos” had me glued to my bed for hours. As I kept turning the pages, I was drawn to another world beyond your regular science fiction. I love the fact that it’s more than that - it’s a hodge podge of topics ranging from Sci-fi, Romance, Action, Adventure, Suspense, Space Travel, Extrasensory powers.<br /><br />Tyler Chase definitely hit the spot with this one! Such brilliant writing! The descriptions and dialogues are so well written I felt like I was right in the middle of the scenes watching as the story unfolds.<br /><br />I always love a good romance story, and Chase did an excellent work taking this novel to a whole new level. The romance between Comron and Vaush was beautifully executed. The warrior in them can clearly be seen even through the toughest circumstances. I was moved beyond doubt that true love can indeed conquer anything.<br /><br />I am in awe really, and still feel goosebumps on my skin as my imagination fires up with every turn of the page. When a novel gives me this much impression and the chance to get my imagination all fired up, I know I have found a keeper! I also believe we found the next Box Office Hit movie!<br /><br />As I turned to the last few pages, Comron’s scenes filled me with so much curiosity. I am impressed with Chaiyse' and Bhedrus’ scheme putting all of them right in the lion’s den so they can be right where they’re supposed to be.<br /> <br />I definitely can’t wait to read Tyler Chase’s next novel. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12199650786798441203" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Tom" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33078013-tom"><img alt="Tom" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1053179755?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tom" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tom" href="/user/show/33078013-tom">Tom</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23119393-van-laven-chronicles">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1053179755" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7347417317121373457">This book really surprised me, in a good way! I judged the book by the title, first of all, and I expected some sort of Game of Thrones knock off, but it is actually really well written and has a very unique storyline, full of action and love. While this is clearly a fiction book, it is worth noting that the author has clearly put a lot of thought, research and effort into this story, and it actually gets better and better throughout the book. <br/>What I really love about this book is how it is acti</span>
  <span id="freeText7347417317121373457" style="display:none">This book really surprised me, in a good way! I judged the book by the title, first of all, and I expected some sort of Game of Thrones knock off, but it is actually really well written and has a very unique storyline, full of action and love. While this is clearly a fiction book, it is worth noting that the author has clearly put a lot of thought, research and effort into this story, and it actually gets better and better throughout the book. <br />What I really love about this book is how it is action filled from the first page to the last - so many books bore me to death for the first ten pages, but this book is full of amazing action scenes, as well as very detailed love scenes. You really get to know the two main characters, Comron and Vaush. Without spoiling anything, I think it is fair to say that I definitely did not see the end coming at all. <br />I also love the mixture of medieval gestures and language, mixed with futuristic space-ships and warfare. It is like a mixture of all my favorite shows/books, yet it is incredibly unique and it keeps you reading chapter after chapter without being bored or wanting to do other things instead. I think one of the reasons for this is the amazing change the main character Comron goes through, and at times I was wondering if this book wasn't written by a man. The author has definitely got a great understanding of the male mind.<br />My favorite part of this book was a scene where the main character Comron was tortured by his evil father for basically following his hearts desires. My least favorite scene was probably the end, just because I wanted it to go on for longer! <br />All in all, this is a great book for anyone who is into a well written love story, set in the future, but very influenced by the past. I can only recommended it!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7347417317121373457" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Stephanie Stevens" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19848949-stephanie-stevens"><img alt="Stephanie Stevens" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367152775p2/19848949.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1054555476?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephanie Stevens" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephanie Stevens" href="/user/show/19848949-stephanie-stevens">Stephanie Stevens</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23119393-van-laven-chronicles">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1054555476" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9648102779536423614">If you are looking for an exciting tale of adventure, intrigue, betrayal, and even love, Van Laven Chronicles: Throne of Novoxos is the perfect book for you. This book captivates the reader from page one and doesn't let go even at the very end. I hope that we will see more books in this series, as there are far more stories to tell.<br/><br/>Author Tyler Chase takes you into the world of futuristic Sci-Fi, while making you feel as if you are reading about 18th Century royal kingdoms. The story revolves ar</span>
  <span id="freeText9648102779536423614" style="display:none">If you are looking for an exciting tale of adventure, intrigue, betrayal, and even love, Van Laven Chronicles: Throne of Novoxos is the perfect book for you. This book captivates the reader from page one and doesn't let go even at the very end. I hope that we will see more books in this series, as there are far more stories to tell.<br /><br />Author Tyler Chase takes you into the world of futuristic Sci-Fi, while making you feel as if you are reading about 18th Century royal kingdoms. The story revolves around Comron, Crown Prince of Nethic and Vaush, of the royal Bastionli family. These two families are sworn enemies and will do anything to keep the other from gaining more power. Comron and Vaush find themselves thrown together after a tragic accident, which was meant to take one of their lives. While they are sworn enemies, they find themselves falling deeply in love and unable to satisfy their longings because of their family's hatred of each other. The couple faces many obstacles on their journey to be together, the worst possibly being Crausin, Comron's father. Crausin has his own demons, which he refuses to face. This is a character you will love to hate, while you try to understand his reasoning for controlling his son. <br /><br />Sci-Fi fans will love the adventure and imagination that Chase brings to life, while romance lovers will become charmed by the couples struggle to be together against their family's wishes. <br /><br />This book is a must read. It will keep you turning pages until the very end. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9648102779536423614" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1058572231" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9779860271072750945">Fabulous book! This book is filled with adventure and romance, which I enjoy a lot. This was the first time that I had read a book by Tyler Chase and what a great author he is. I loved the storyline and the characters. The book is also very well-written. When I first started to read it, I knew that it would be a book that I wouldn't be able to set down. I never did and I ended up finishing the book in one setting. The cover is really what drew me to the book, it gave the promise of adventure and</span>
  <span id="freeText9779860271072750945" style="display:none">Fabulous book! This book is filled with adventure and romance, which I enjoy a lot. This was the first time that I had read a book by Tyler Chase and what a great author he is. I loved the storyline and the characters. The book is also very well-written. When I first started to read it, I knew that it would be a book that I wouldn't be able to set down. I never did and I ended up finishing the book in one setting. The cover is really what drew me to the book, it gave the promise of adventure and there was a ton of it. Once I read the description I decided to give the book a try.<br /><br />Comron is willing to go through extreme measures in order to get what he desires and he will not stop until he has conquered all. He encounters Vaush and he falls madly in love with her, but little does he realize that his enemies are trying to destroy his kingdom through her. Comron and his dark secrets come about. His family secrets are also out and haunting him. Comron is torn between his love for Vaush and trying to save his kingdom; it’s a very difficult situation for him. He is a heir and won't let anything come between him and his kingdom. It was very interesting to see Comron balance his love for Vaush and try to protect his kingdom from the enemies. Sometimes the enemies within are more dangerous than the enemies on the outside. Read this one, it is worth it. <br /></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7621920791809464074">Van Laven Chronicles: Throne of Novoxos is one of the best books I have ever read. I usually don't read science fiction/fantasy books but I gave this one a try. As soon as I started reading it, I just kept going! Tyler Chase's style of writing kept my interest from the beginning. Chase is an amazing author. Plus this book packs romance and action-adventure. I'm so glad I read it.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1066637583" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1066637583" />
    <a title="jessica Woods" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7717019-jessica-woods"><img alt="jessica Woods" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1066637583?book_show_action=true">Sep 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jessica Woods" class="user" itemprop="url" name="jessica Woods" href="/user/show/7717019-jessica-woods">jessica Woods</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1066637583" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17502867247658073589">I didn't want to like this book. A few pages in, I wondered why I was reading it, when there didn't seem to be any clear genre in mind. But, I kept reading, and before I knew it, I was hooked.<br/><br/>Like a train wreck you can't look away from, I had to keep reading to find out exactly what the heck was really going on with the characters in the story. The main characters were in turns repugnant and compelling, particularly Comron. He vacillated between misogynistic pig and hopeless romantic, and I foun</span>
  <span id="freeText17502867247658073589" style="display:none">I didn't want to like this book. A few pages in, I wondered why I was reading it, when there didn't seem to be any clear genre in mind. But, I kept reading, and before I knew it, I was hooked.<br /><br />Like a train wreck you can't look away from, I had to keep reading to find out exactly what the heck was really going on with the characters in the story. The main characters were in turns repugnant and compelling, particularly Comron. He vacillated between misogynistic pig and hopeless romantic, and I found his character flaws endearing.<br /><br />Vaush was a little less defined, in my opinion, but I loved her tenacity. I kept seeing Kathleen Turner in the "Romancing the Stone" film when I read her...she was feisty!<br /><br />I had a bit of a hard time keeping up with the political aspects of the story...partly because the universe of the book was so vast. I did enjoy the twists and turns, particularly the last third of the book, when creepy revelations are made and certain horrid characters show themselves to be truly evil.<br /><br />There was a lot of aggression against the female characters, but it was in keeping with the twisted psyche of the male antagonist. <br /><br />This was a surprisingly good read, and I look forward to seeing how the author continues the story. I was hoping for a happy ending, and it looks like it could still happen, but I guess I'll have to wait for the next book to find out.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17502867247658073589" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1786931144" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1786931144" />
    <a title="Shay Williams" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2618606-shay-williams"><img alt="Shay Williams" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1250657433p2/2618606.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1786931144?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shay Williams" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shay Williams" href="/user/show/2618606-shay-williams">Shay Williams</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2618606-shay-williams?shelf=net-galley">net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2618606-shay-williams?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2618606-shay-williams?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1786931144" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1874509846360139129">I so love a good space opera filled with space and land battles, impossible relationship and interstellar politics. And I do have to say that the THRONE OF NOVOXOS has all of those and more. <br/><br/> <br/><br/>When I first started reading the book and met Comron I was immediately taken back to Dune but that impression didn't last for long. While there are politics, they seem to be more approachable then the ones in the old sci-fi standby. And to tell you the truth, I found Comron to be a bit of an ass. I know tha</span>
  <span id="freeText1874509846360139129" style="display:none">I so love a good space opera filled with space and land battles, impossible relationship and interstellar politics. And I do have to say that the THRONE OF NOVOXOS has all of those and more. <br /><br /> <br /><br />When I first started reading the book and met Comron I was immediately taken back to Dune but that impression didn't last for long. While there are politics, they seem to be more approachable then the ones in the old sci-fi standby. And to tell you the truth, I found Comron to be a bit of an ass. I know that a good portion of that is his upbringing by his insane father but still.<br /><br /> <br /><br />The character that I really liked is the one that Comron fell in love with Vaush. She is down to earth and just wants to make the world, or in this case worlds, a better place for everyone to live. So of course she saves Comron even though their families are deadly enemies because that is the type of person she is.<br /><br /> <br /><br />I really enjoyed THRONE OF NOVOXOS with its fast pacing, interesting characters, an unauthorized love and danger around every turn. I do think that my readers who enjoy space opera will enjoy it. There are a few sex scenes but nothing too graphic so this book would work for older teens as well as adults.<br /><br /><br />*** I received this book at no charge from NetGalley in exchange for a fair and honest review. All opinions expressed within are my own.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1874509846360139129" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1063230763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4425048716653760873">Van Laven Chronicles: Throne of Novoxos is a unique story full of love and war, masterfully pieced together by author Tyler Chase. Comron and Vaush, the two main characters, capture the heart of readers from the beginning of the story and keep you enraptured through every surprise, and trust me, there are many twists and turns in store. Warning: there are very graphic love scenes that will leave you feigning over Prince Comron, keeping you hooked and committed till the final page. These scenes a</span>
  <span id="freeText4425048716653760873" style="display:none">Van Laven Chronicles: Throne of Novoxos is a unique story full of love and war, masterfully pieced together by author Tyler Chase. Comron and Vaush, the two main characters, capture the heart of readers from the beginning of the story and keep you enraptured through every surprise, and trust me, there are many twists and turns in store. Warning: there are very graphic love scenes that will leave you feigning over Prince Comron, keeping you hooked and committed till the final page. These scenes are balanced out by epic battles and wars, full of danger. Throw in the psychological frenzy of the Van Laven men and you will never be disappointed! Each page was another thrill and another wild fantasy. <br /><br />We follow the characters as they grow together and separate, eventually stumbling into a secret so big that it could literally lead to life or death. Just when you think you can predict what will happen next, Chase reveals a new dimension of the story line, accumulating into an epic enthralling adventure. Forbidden love and political struggles are the main themes that run through the pages of the story. I could not put this book down and can't wait for more of the Van Laven Chronicles!</span>

<div id="review_2185478618" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2185478618" />
    <a title="Robyn Powley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45609292-robyn-powley"><img alt="Robyn Powley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448636605p2/45609292.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2185478618?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robyn Powley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robyn Powley" href="/user/show/45609292-robyn-powley">Robyn Powley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2185478618" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer755500581977758758">I was so happy to receive The Throne of Novoxos by Tyler Chase, from the publisher to read and review. Being a debut novel, I didn’t expect such a tightly-paced, enthralling sci-fi adventure, with all the high octane of a good space opera mixed with sizzling splash of soap opera. <br/><br/>The author takes the premise of Romeo and Juliet as a skeletal background, then proceeds to flesh out the main characters of Vaush and Comron with intelligence, energy, and sex-appeal. <br/><br/>The galaxy Chase has created is po</span>
  <span id="freeText755500581977758758" style="display:none">I was so happy to receive The Throne of Novoxos by Tyler Chase, from the publisher to read and review. Being a debut novel, I didn’t expect such a tightly-paced, enthralling sci-fi adventure, with all the high octane of a good space opera mixed with sizzling splash of soap opera. <br /><br />The author takes the premise of Romeo and Juliet as a skeletal background, then proceeds to flesh out the main characters of Vaush and Comron with intelligence, energy, and sex-appeal. <br /><br />The galaxy Chase has created is populated by interesting, multifaceted individuals, with Comron being one of the most complex, enigmatic protagonists I’ve ever experienced. Though charismatic and smart, he can be both heroic and villainous. His actions are not always likeable, but his motivations are generally pure, at least to the time and place that he exists within. This guy is unique—by any measure—and that makes the story mesmerizing. <br /><br />Except for the inevitable rivals-falling-in-love, I never knew what to expect, which meant I couldn’t put the book down. The action was immersive. The sex was scorching. The science and technology never bogged the story down. Having just finished the story, I now have to get the second book in the trilogy because I really MUST find out what happens next. <br /><br />The Throne of Novoxos is a character-driven action story that happens to take place in another galaxy. It is the best type of science fiction.</span>
  <a data-text-id="755500581977758758" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Mr. Chase is a magician of the written word because this world and the people in it that he has created for us are amazing and fantastical.   <span id="freeText17726957351717076222" style="display:none">Loved it! <br /><br />This book has had me in its grip for the last 2 days and wouldn’t let me go. Every character has been perfectly created to mesh together and bring all nuances of their parts of the story to life. Mr. Chase is a magician of the written word because this world and the people in it that he has created for us are amazing and fantastical. The twists that Mr. Chase throws at you are mind bending and with just enough intrigue it keeps you from putting the book down. I could not recommend this book any higher, if you read nothing else this year, Please Read This One!!!!         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14222956501048642953"><strong>Fantastical</strong><br/><br/>Be prepared for a long read. With that being said,let me add also,be prepared for a great read.<br/>Even though,there is not any given dates,you can deduct that,this is way in the future. Also,it could be in one of the newly discovered galaxies. So,basically,a futuristic Romeo and Juliet story. Two families,a struggle for reign and power. The heir to one throne, and the free spirited,warrior daughter of the other. They find themselves in a dire situation,when their transport is shot down,C</span>
  <span id="freeText14222956501048642953" style="display:none"><strong>Fantastical</strong><br /><br />Be prepared for a long read. With that being said,let me add also,be prepared for a great read.<br />Even though,there is not any given dates,you can deduct that,this is way in the future. Also,it could be in one of the newly discovered galaxies. So,basically,a futuristic Romeo and Juliet story. Two families,a struggle for reign and power. The heir to one throne, and the free spirited,warrior daughter of the other. They find themselves in a dire situation,when their transport is shot down,Comron is wounded gravely,Vaush is tempted to leave him to die,after all he and his house are murdering brutes.Something compels her to help him,hoping she'll be long gone,by the time he wakes up. As fate would have it,that doesn't happen. We all know what happens now. Unbeknownst to her,Comrons father is mad,not just angry,but a deranged sociopathic psycho. He will do whatever it takes to keep his test tube experiment on homeland. Unbeknownst to Vaush,she is the heir to the one throne that can either end them all or bring them together. The odds are not in their favor,and lies, and misleading, and some blind trust, must be given and earned,if the plan will work. Will love conquer all? I will say by the last line,I was wondering myself. For this kind of book to be written by a woman,in a male dominated genre,it was a true surprise,at how this first book in Tyler's series,blew others I have read out of the water. Was not farfetched,or unbelievable,a book you can actually see in your minds eye.</span>

<div id="review_1819820785" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1819820785" />
    <a title="Jolie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5122879-jolie"><img alt="Jolie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450230193p2/5122879.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1819820785?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jolie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jolie" href="/user/show/5122879-jolie">Jolie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4345855064512167375">Another example of me judging a book by its cover/blurb. I really need to stop doing that because I always end up making a fool out of myself when talking through the review with my husband….sigh.<br/><br/>This is a Romeo and Juliet type love story coupled with some good old-fashioned science fiction and fantasy elements mixed in. The only way that it differs from Romeo and Juliet is that Comron and Vaush do not die a star cross lovers death. They come close a few times but they don’t die.<br/><br/>Comron and his f</span>
  <span id="freeText4345855064512167375" style="display:none">Another example of me judging a book by its cover/blurb. I really need to stop doing that because I always end up making a fool out of myself when talking through the review with my husband….sigh.<br /><br />This is a Romeo and Juliet type love story coupled with some good old-fashioned science fiction and fantasy elements mixed in. The only way that it differs from Romeo and Juliet is that Comron and Vaush do not die a star cross lovers death. They come close a few times but they don’t die.<br /><br />Comron and his father, Crausin, have one of the most complex and, dare I say, disgusting relationships in the books that I have read in the past few years. They telepathic, which was fascinating, especially something major was revealed to Vaush from Comron towards the end of the story. They didn’t use their telepathy to always talk to each other. Crausin used it to take over while Comron is having sex. So, a telepathic threesome. They also shared their women in the physical sense too. A father/son threesome….gag. I should add that Crausin is the Grand Duke of the planet Nethic and Comron is the Crown Prince. So yeah….lol.<br /><br />Vaush is the youngest daughter of Larrs Bastionli, the Duke of Tir-Laros and Comron and Crausin’s mortal enemy. She is a woman who loves nothing more than to stay out of her father’s path and do what she loves….helping others less fortunate than her.<br /><br />Vaush and Comron’s paths cross when the transport that she is on (that is also carrying members a delegation that is selling security technology and the investors interested in it.) is attacked by a terrorist. A bomb explodes, causing the transport to crash. Vaush is largely uninjured (we do find out why later on in the book) but Comron is gravely injured. Vaush finds him in the wreckage, discovers who he is and decides to save him (remember, their planets are mortal enemies and they are honor bound to kill each other). Comron returns the favor after a panther attacks Vaush in the jungle.<br /><br />While they are trekking towards the east coast, and hopefully rescue, Vaush and Comron fall in love and do the dirty. They vow to keep seeing each other, on the down low, after they are rescued.<br /><br />Once they are rescued, a huge secret about Vaush comes to light. She is the legal heir of the Emperor’s throne. The Emperor took her mother as his first wife, much to the dismay of his ex-wife and their children. When her mother got pregnant, she disappeared and was assumed to have died….this child along with her. Which wasn’t the case. Her transport was waylaid by Larrs Bastionli, her mother severely injured but kept alive to deliver Vaush and then was either killed or died after her birth. Larrs kept Vaush and raised her as his own child but with it always in the back of his head that one day, when she old enough, that she will become the Empress and Tir-Laros will have the backing of the Empress.<br /><br />Only, it didn’t quite turn out that way. There is murder and mayhem once her secret is leaked. The only true ally that Vaush has is Comron but even that is questioned when huge secrets from his past are revealed to her.<br /><br />I never thought that I would ever say this in a science fiction/fantasy but the sex scenes are insanely good. Each sex scene was better than the next. I loved it!!<br /><br />The ending of the book threw me for a loop and made me question Comron and his loyalty to Vaush. There were other instances that made me go “Eh” but when I read what I read at the end, I went “Ooooooo….no he didn’t!!” I am actually going to buy the 2nd book because I want to know what happens next.<br /><br />**I chose to leave this review after reading an advance reader copy**</span>

          </span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15784017-online-eccentric-librarian?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15784017-online-eccentric-librarian?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15784017-online-eccentric-librarian?shelf=romance">romance</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1732719545" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6265818843018315500"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399322283i/9534702.jpg' alt='More reviews at the Online Eccentric Librarian http://surrealtalvi.wordpress.com/' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <p>
  <i>More reviews (and no fluff) on the blog <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://surrealtalvi.wordpress.com/'>http://surrealtalvi.wordpress.com/</a></i>
</p>Admittedly, I had a hard time with this novel. Both the plot and the writing trod well worn tropes without really utilizing the sci fi setting. Characters were flat as cardboard, with the evil being eeeevil and the good so over-the-top angelic that I'd expect little birds to brush their hair in the morning. Alpha overbearing male lead, sweet and innocent (with a hidden past!) heroine, and a lot of undeveloped extras m</span>
  <span id="freeText6265818843018315500" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399322283i/9534702.jpg" alt="More reviews at the Online Eccentric Librarian http://surrealtalvi.wordpress.com/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <p>
  <i>More reviews (and no fluff) on the blog <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://surrealtalvi.wordpress.com/">http://surrealtalvi.wordpress.com/</a></i>
</p>Admittedly, I had a hard time with this novel. Both the plot and the writing trod well worn tropes without really utilizing the sci fi setting. Characters were flat as cardboard, with the evil being eeeevil and the good so over-the-top angelic that I'd expect little birds to brush their hair in the morning. Alpha overbearing male lead, sweet and innocent (with a hidden past!) heroine, and a lot of undeveloped extras make up the bulk of this story.<br><br>The writing was especially bland - within the first few pages we get clunky and cliche'd sentences such as these:<br><br>"I cannot be certain until we've interrogated the survivors. If House Bastionli is behind this, they will pay dearly for their meddling."<br><br>"He jumped up onto the execution platform and retrieved the ostako swords still dripping with blood and bits of flesh."<br><br>"...he stood nearly a head taller than most men and possessed a fierce look in his striking green eyes, while his raven-black hair contrasted sharply against his fair skin..."<br><br>Pretty much most of the plot is telegraphed and there aren't any real surprises. Even by idealistic standards, this is fairy tale fluffy with some rather violent/aggressive sex thrown in. The sci fi aspects serve only so we can have royalty but not with the usual medieval fantasy trapping. They don't really add to the story at all since the story is very generic.<br><br>Undemanding readers of the romance genre will find this to be a nice little time killer. But readers of the sci fi genre especially will likely be frustrated by the lack of depth and nuance.<br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1061454441" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1061454441" />
    <a title="Sharla Shotwell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12996625-sharla-shotwell"><img alt="Sharla Shotwell" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1061454441?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharla Shotwell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharla Shotwell" href="/user/show/12996625-sharla-shotwell">Sharla Shotwell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23119393-van-laven-chronicles">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1061454441" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4365882896844718618">Tyler Chase, the author of this book is an amazing writer. His brilliance is shown within the pages of this work. I love the way he starts mid-stream at the beginning of the story. A story that has tones somewhat akin though unrelated to the popular show “Game of Thrones,” or the true stories of "The Crusades," only more original in concept and thought. <br/><br/>It is interesting that Tyler includes two different aspects of spectators in an arena, some wanting to kill and others wanting to save a prisone</span>
  <span id="freeText4365882896844718618" style="display:none">Tyler Chase, the author of this book is an amazing writer. His brilliance is shown within the pages of this work. I love the way he starts mid-stream at the beginning of the story. A story that has tones somewhat akin though unrelated to the popular show “Game of Thrones,” or the true stories of "The Crusades," only more original in concept and thought. <br /><br />It is interesting that Tyler includes two different aspects of spectators in an arena, some wanting to kill and others wanting to save a prisoner or prisoners from the sword. The emphasis on imagery in the story paints a clear picture for readers in which one begins to envision actually being present in the arena during these dramatic tribunals. <br /><br />Intriguing would be an understatement. Upon reading the book, I immediately became enthralled with the storyline which kept me wanting to continue to read on throughout the entire story. <br /><br />It is not often one finds such a suspenseful story these days. A story full of royalty, including Kings &amp; Queens, prisoners and countrymen, guards and traitors. As a result, drama, espionage, and suspense are also quite present. All in all, this is a very well written and thought out storyline. <br /><br />I would highly recommend this book to all those who enjoy overwhelming drama and suspense in realms of royalty. The overall plot is powerfully beautiful though horrid with excellent imagery and justice which override the demise for the prisoners in the beginning. <br /><br />By the end of the story, the reader finds oneself questioning where one would stand if present at the time the prisoners were being beheaded. And, where one might go forth from this make believe city of pain and torture, forgiveness and rebirth. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4365882896844718618" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1068977461" />
    <a title="Niyati Em" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25492176-niyati-em"><img alt="Niyati Em" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1068977461?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Niyati Em" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Niyati Em" href="/user/show/25492176-niyati-em">Niyati Em</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1068977461" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3720690605947975061">When I started reading this book, I thought it would be another one of those where the two characters would meet and then fall in love and they would fight. I thought it would take a romantic turn and be a cliche!!<br/><br/>BUT NO! I couldn't have been more wrong.<br/><br/>This book had so much of depth and twists and turns at every moment.<br/><br/>I was so hooked on to the book. It was lengthy, I must admit, but having said that, there were twists at every step which made me want to find out what happened next. The whole j</span>
  <span id="freeText3720690605947975061" style="display:none">When I started reading this book, I thought it would be another one of those where the two characters would meet and then fall in love and they would fight. I thought it would take a romantic turn and be a cliche!!<br /><br />BUT NO! I couldn't have been more wrong.<br /><br />This book had so much of depth and twists and turns at every moment.<br /><br />I was so hooked on to the book. It was lengthy, I must admit, but having said that, there were twists at every step which made me want to find out what happened next. The whole journey from their rescue to the events that transpire next, really brought a futuristic world in front of me.<br /><br />What I loved about this book was that the characters had back stories. Comron had a story about his creation. Crausin had his own mental problems and Vaush has a whole lot of problems coming her way. They all have a life apart from their royal duties. They have their vices, weaknesses and their pleasures. It made the characters so much more believable.<br /><br />I felt some connection to Vaush. She was an admirable character. She made me root for her and her relationship with Comron. I felt Comron and Crausin's insanity really scary and I felt the whole political upturn happening during the book to be interesting. <br /><br />I can't be more straightforward when I say, I WANT THE NEXT BOOK. I just want it now!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3720690605947975061" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="H. Bloom" class="user" itemprop="url" name="H. Bloom" href="/user/show/35313115-h-bloom">H. Bloom</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1275769755" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5209008802410583749">A few months ago I read “Shadow Reign”, Book 2 in the Van Laven Chronicles series. I had so much great fun reading it, despite the fact I started the series out of order, that the moment I finished reading it I knew I wanted to go back and read Book 1 of the series. And I wasn’t disappointed at all. “Van Laren Chronicles: Throne of Novoxos” is a great read. The story-line is ever-evolving. It’s deep in character and plot line development, full of suspense, sinister foreshadowing and shocking rev</span>
  <span id="freeText5209008802410583749" style="display:none">A few months ago I read “Shadow Reign”, Book 2 in the Van Laven Chronicles series. I had so much great fun reading it, despite the fact I started the series out of order, that the moment I finished reading it I knew I wanted to go back and read Book 1 of the series. And I wasn’t disappointed at all. “Van Laren Chronicles: Throne of Novoxos” is a great read. The story-line is ever-evolving. It’s deep in character and plot line development, full of suspense, sinister foreshadowing and shocking revelations.<br />The male lead is Prince Comron Van Laven of Nethic. Comron has to sacrifice himself so Nethic may gain a seat on the Imperial Reserve Board and a place among the Great Houses. He has been betrothed to a woman he doesn’t love. He also has serious father issues. There are two powerful female characters in this book: Vaush Bastionli of Ti-Laros, and Lady Spira Eskridge. But who is his real love? And whose father is the diabolically insane one? <br />A major twist of plot occurs in the middle of the book and no one is who they appear to be.<br />If you get this book, then be prepared to lose some sleep because you won’t be able to wait to find out what the answers to these questions are.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5209008802410583749" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hammad Tahir" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hammad Tahir" href="/user/show/37138869-hammad-tahir">Hammad Tahir</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1114992639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12436753582140988163">Van Laven Chronicles is one of the finest books I have ever read. I usually don't peruse science fiction/fantasy books, but I went for this one because it is really an exception among the fiction writings. I couldn't stop reading it once I started because the beginning of the story was so captivating that it kept me going on. Tyler Chase's style of writing is just amazing and it keeps the most interesting perspective of the topic above all. Chase is a professional author and knows how to write a</span>
  <span id="freeText12436753582140988163" style="display:none">Van Laven Chronicles is one of the finest books I have ever read. I usually don't peruse science fiction/fantasy books, but I went for this one because it is really an exception among the fiction writings. I couldn't stop reading it once I started because the beginning of the story was so captivating that it kept me going on. Tyler Chase's style of writing is just amazing and it keeps the most interesting perspective of the topic above all. Chase is a professional author and knows how to write a fiction. This book covers romance and action adventure side by side and keeps the story parts in great order. Overall, its a great book and I recommend it to readers of every age group. Great work Tyler Chase. </span>

<div id="review_1772828571" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1772828571" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5196121-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485755158p2/5196121.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1772828571?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/5196121-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1772828571" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12891728895089057362">This is absolutely the best book I've read in a long time. It's one I could pick right back up and read over again back to back, and hopefully get some sleep along the way since that didn't happen the first time through. It's packed full of action, romance and suspense, with unexpected twists and turns. As the opener to a trilogy, it sets the stage and buries the hook for book two, which I'll be reading next. <br/>Copy received in return for an honest review. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1676339969" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Raina Collins" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11801213-raina-collins"><img alt="Raina Collins" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421876744p2/11801213.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1676339969?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Raina Collins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Raina Collins" href="/user/show/11801213-raina-collins">Raina Collins</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1676339969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18207198531513466920">Received through NetGalley for an honest review. <br/><br/>This is a very intense book filled with political agendas. The main characters are like Romeo and Juliet but they aren't about to give up their lives easily no matter what happens with their families. The battles are fought in space and on alien planets. The main agenda for the families is power. But love is all the main characters really want. </span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9x+l/SJQjR1qi6bSZChYH2ZyIyh0Ll7aOERZ/HU1rqce/N0Bc+K3pYsl9q6D9dDNAVGzTnXVghCYK7e/f0ItSw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vxKl2xZGZZdPUg2+Bb6aSewEUgsMNZDKC3AIenujQ5pW8d0nR/RfL678XcLiYxKbiyfCbQ3OTACrH+Y5cdTAdg==')})
  }
//]]>

Roosevelt’s death. Countdown 1945 tells the gripping true story of the turbulent days, weeks, and months to follow, leading up to August 6, 1945, when new President Harry Truman gives the order to unleash the world’s first atomic bomb. Featuring some of history’s most remarkable leaders, page-turning action, and vivid details, Countdown 1945 is a thrilling narrative of the covert meetings and pivotal developments that took place in the United States and around the world during the volatile spring and summer of 1945.\n\nCountdown 1945 takes readers inside the minds of the iconic and elusive figures who join the quest for the bomb, each for different reasons: the legendary Albert Einstein, who eventually calls his vocal support for the atomic bomb “the one great mistake in my life”; lead researcher Robert “Oppie” Oppenheimer and the Soviet spies who secretly infiltrate his team; the fiercely competitive pilots of the plane selected to drop the bomb; and many more. Perhaps most of all, Countdown 1945 is the story of an untested new president confronting a decision that he knows will change the world forever. Truman’s journey during these 116 days is a story of high drama: from the shock of learning of the bomb’s existence, to the conflicting advice he receives from generals like Eisenhower and George Marshall, to wrestling with the devastating carnage that will result if he gives the order to use America’s first weapon of mass destruction.\n\nBut Countdown 1945 is more than a book about the atomic bomb. It’s also an unforgettable account of the lives of ordinary American and Japanese civilians in wartime—from “Calutron Girls” like Ruth Sisson in Oak Ridge, Tennessee, to ten-year-old Hiroshima resident Hideko Tamura, who survives the blast at ground zero but loses her mother, and later immigrates to the United States, where she lives to this day—as well as American soldiers fighting in the Pacific, waiting in fear for the order to launch a possible invasion of Japan. Told with vigor, intelligence, and humanity, Countdown 1945 is the definitive account of one of the most consequential moments in history.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"13773905207014791872\"
